RUS_setup_senate_duma_conflict_variables = {
	set_temp_variable = { bop_value = mp_support }
	divide_temp_variable = { bop_value = 550 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = bop_value
				value = 0.5
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			divide_temp_variable = { bop_value = -2 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		multiply_temp_variable = { bop_value = 2 }
	}
		
	set_power_balance = {
		id = RUS_senate_duma_conflict
		left_side = RUS_duma_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		right_side = RUS_senate_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		#set_default = yes # whether or not to reset the power balance to the initial value, default = no
		set_value = var:bop_value # if specified will set the value of the power balance, this option will override the effect of set_default so the two options should not be used together. if neither set_default or set_value is specified the current value of the power balance will not change
	}	
}
RUS_bop_low_increase_effect_10 = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = RUS_senate_duma_conflict
		value = 0.10
	}
}

	add_power_balance_value = {

		value = 0.12
	}

RUS_calculate_government_variables = {	
}
RUS_add_to_coalition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition }
		add_synd_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^1 = 1 } # PLSR  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition }
		add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^2 = 1 } # NSP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition }
		add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^3 = 1 } # PSR  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition }
		add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^4 = 1 } # RSDRP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition }
		add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^5 = 1 } # LKDP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = progressive_coalition }
		add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^6 = 1 } # PP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition }
		add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^7 = 1 } # RKDP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition }
		add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
		add_authdem_to_coalition = yes		
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^8 = 1 } # VNS  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition }
		add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^9 = 1 } # EP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition }
		add_natpop_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^12 = 1 } # NRPR  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition }
		add_natpop_to_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^11 = 1 } # NSNP  (Governing)		
	}	
}
RUS_remove_from_coalition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
		clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition_to_remove
		remove_synd_from_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^1 = 3 } # PLSR  (Opposition)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
		clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition_to_remove
		remove_radsoc_from_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^2 = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = psr_coalition
		clr_country_flag = psr_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^3 = 3 }
		remove_socdem_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition_to_remove }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^4 = 3 }
		remove_socdem_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
		clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^5 = 3 }
		remove_soclib_from_coalition = yes
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = progressive_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = progressive_coalition
		clr_country_flag = progressive_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^6 = 3 } #
		remove_marlib_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
		clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^7 = 3 }
		remove_marlib_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
		clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^8 = 3 }
		remove_soccon_from_coalition = yes
		remove_authdem_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
		clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^9 = 3 }
		remove_authdem_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition_to_remove }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^12 = 3 }
		remove_natpop_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition_to_remove }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^11 = 3 }
		remove_natpop_from_coalition = yes
	}	
}

RUS_psr_rrdo = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		RUS_dissolve_kdp_and_make_rkdp_pp = yes
	}
	add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^3 = Duma_Party_Seats^5 }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = 0 }
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
	remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
	mp_support_calc = yes 
	senators_support_calc = yes	
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_integrate_lkdp_full
	hidden_effect = {
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@social_democrat}
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@social_liberal  }

		set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = RUS_new_socdem }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = sum } #avoid rounding errors

		set_popularities = {
			totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
			syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
			radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
			social_democrat = RUS_new_socdem
			social_liberal = 0
			market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
			social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
			authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
			paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
			national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
		}
	}
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_minister_for = token:RUS_Nikolay_V_Nekrasov_for_sli }
	remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
	add_ideas = RUS_Nikolay_V_Nekrasov_for_sli
}
RUS_psr_rpr = {
	clr_country_flag = nsnp_banned
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = national_populist
		name = RUS_solidarist_party
		long_name = RUS_solidarist_party_long
	}
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^11 = Duma_Party_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^11 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^11 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^12 }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^11 = 0.4 }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^11 = 0.4 }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^11 = 0.4 }
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^11
	round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^11
	round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^11
	subtract_from_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^12 = Duma_Party_Seats^11 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^12 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^11 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^12 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^11 }
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
			multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 0.4 }
			multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.6 }
		}
	}		
	add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^3 = Duma_Party_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^12 = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^12 = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^12 = 0 }
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
	remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
	mp_support_calc = yes 
	senators_support_calc = yes	
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_integrate_nrpr_half
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = rusdem.204
			days = 30
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_new_natpop = RUS.party_popularity_100@national_populist }
		divide_temp_variable = { RUS_new_natpop = 2 }

		set_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = RUS.party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = RUS_new_natpop }

		set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = RUS_new_socdem }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = RUS_new_natpop }

		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_new_socdem = sum } #avoid rounding errors

		set_popularities = {
			totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
			syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
			radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
			social_democrat = RUS_new_socdem
			social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
			market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
			social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
			authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
			paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
			national_populist = RUS_new_natpop
		}
	}
}

RUS_dissolve_kdp_and_make_rkdp_pp = {
	clr_country_flag = kdp_united
	set_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_progressives
	clr_country_flag = pp_banned
	clr_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_kdp_progressives
	set_country_flag = rkdp_banned
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_vote }
	add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = 550 }
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^5
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^6
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_vote }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_senate_vote }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = 550 }
	round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^5
	round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^6
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = 550 }
	round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5
	round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		name = RUS_progressive_party
		long_name = RUS_progressive_party_long
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes 
	senators_support_calc = yes	
}
RUS_dissolve_kdp_into_three = {
	clr_country_flag = kdp_united
	set_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_progressives
	set_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_ldp
	set_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdp
	clr_country_flag = pp_banned
	clr_country_flag = rkdp_banned
	clr_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_kdp_progressives
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^7 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^7 = 550 }
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^5
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^6
	round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^7
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_elections_senate_1936 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 }
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 }
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = 0 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = 0 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 }
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 }
		add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = 0 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = 0 }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 = 0 }
		remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_vote }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_senate_vote }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 = 50 }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = 50 }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 = 50 }
		round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^5
		round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^6
		round_variable = Senate_Party_General_Seats^7
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
		set_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 = 50 }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = 50 }
		multiply_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 = 50 }
		round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5
		round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6
		round_variable = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7
		remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { 
				has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			name = RUS_rrdp_party
			long_name = RUS_rrdp_party_long
		}
	}
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		name = RUS_ldp_party
		long_name = RUS_ldp_party_long
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes 
	senators_support_calc = yes	
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
}
RUS_dissolve_rkdp_into_two = {
	clr_country_flag = pp_banned
	set_country_flag = rkdp_banned
	set_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_progressives
	clr_country_flag = RUS_marlibs_ldp
	# Duma seats
	set_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	multiply_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = 275 }
	round_temp_variable = rkdp_pp_faction
	subtract_from_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^7 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Duma_Part_Seats^8 = Duma_Party_Seats^7 }
	
	# Senate seats
	set_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_vote }
	multiply_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = 25 }
	round_temp_variable = rkdp_pp_faction
	subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^6 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^8 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 }
	
	set_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	multiply_temp_variable = { rkdp_pp_faction = 25 }
	round_temp_variable = rkdp_pp_faction
	subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^6 = rkdp_pp_faction }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^8 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 }
	
	remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
	set_party_name = {
		ideology = market_liberal
		name = RUS_progressive_party
		long_name = RUS_progressive_party_long
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes 
	senators_support_calc = yes	
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
}
RUS_clear_all_coalitions = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Status
		value = status
		index = i

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { status = 1 } } # Coalition
			set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 3 }
		}
	}
	end_coalition = yes
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
}

RUS_setup_initial_state_popularities = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_owned_by = RUS
					is_core_of = RUS
				}
				# Eastern Europe #
				is_owned_by = FIN
				is_owned_by = BAT
				is_owned_by = LIT
				is_owned_by = POL
				is_owned_by = GAL
				is_owned_by = WHR
				is_owned_by = UKR
				state = 78
				state = 1222
				state = 1320
				# Don-Kuban #
				is_owned_by = KUB
				is_owned_by = DKB
				is_owned_by = KLY
				# Caucasus #
				is_owned_by = MTR
				is_owned_by = AZE
				is_owned_by = GEO
				is_owned_by = ARM
				# Central Asia #
				is_owned_by = ALO
				is_owned_by = KYR
				is_owned_by = TRK
				is_owned_by = UZB
				# Far-East #
				is_owned_by = TRM
				is_owned_by = MON
				state = 537
				state = 555
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_party_pop_states_array = THIS }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_general_turnout = 0.7 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_senate_turnout = 0.3 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout = 0.2 }
		set_variable = { RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout = 6 }
		#RUS_clamp_all_state_pop = yes
		RUS_generate_state_popularities = yes
	}
}
RUS_generate_state_popularities = { #Fires at game start, and when absorbing colonies
	# Main Parties #
	
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@totalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@syndicalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	if = {
		limit = { PREV = { tag = RUS} }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@social_liberal }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@social_liberal }
		#Adjust for PSR/RSDRP
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.5 }
	}
	#set_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = PREV.party_popularity@national_populist }
	
	#Adjust for VNS, EP
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_ep_vns_fraction = RUS_state_ep_popularity }	
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_ep_vns_fraction = 0.7 }
		
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = RUS_state_ep_vns_fraction }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS_state_ep_vns_fraction }
		
	#Adjust for KDP, NSNP
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_pp_fraction = RUS_state_lkdp_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_pp_fraction = RUS_state_rkdp_popularity }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_pp_fraction = 0.2 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_pp_fraction = 0.4 }
		
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = RUS_state_lkdp_pp_fraction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = RUS_state_rkdp_pp_fraction }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS_state_lkdp_pp_fraction }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = RUS_state_rkdp_pp_fraction }
	
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 0.2 }
		
	# Non-Partisan #
	set_variable = { RUS_state_autonomists_popularity = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_popularity = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0 }
	
	#Adjust for ROVS
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_monarchists_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_independent_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_monarchists_fraction = 0.3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_independent_fraction = 0.3 }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_monarchists_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_monarchists_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_independent_fraction }
	}	
	#Adjust for Organisations
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_independent_faction = RUS_state_plsr_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_independent_faction = RUS_state_nsp_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_psr_independent_faction = RUS_state_psr_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_independent_faction = RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_independent_faction = RUS_state_lkdp_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_independent_faction = RUS_state_rkdp_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_vns_independent_faction = RUS_state_vns_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_ep_independent_faction = RUS_state_ep_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_independent_faction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_independent_faction = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
	
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_psr_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_vns_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_ep_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_independent_faction = 0.03 }
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_plsr_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_nsp_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_psr_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_rsdrp_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_lkdp_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_rkdp_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_vns_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_ep_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_independent_faction }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_independent_faction }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_vns_monarchists_fraction = RUS_state_vns_popularity }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_vns_monarchists_fraction = 0.10 }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_monarchists_popularity = RUS_state_vns_monarchists_fraction }
		
	#Defining temporary state pop variables (to be reset by election)
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_autonomists_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_monarchists_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }
	
	RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = yes
	
}
RUS_adjusted_state_pops = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.03 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.06 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_socdem_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0.08 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 1.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				OR = {
					tag = FIN
					tag = EST
					tag = LIT
					tag = ALO
					tag = KYR
					tag = UZB
					tag = TRK
					tag = ARM
					tag = GEO
					tag = AZE
					tag = CRM
				}
			}
		}	
		set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_popularity = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0 }
	}	
}
RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = {
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_pp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_autonomists_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_monarchists_condition_pop = 0 }
	
	#Industry makes states more leftist
	set_temp_variable = { industrial_popularity = THIS.num_of_factories }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 10 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.125 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 9 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.10 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 8 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.075 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 7 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 6 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.025 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 5 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 3 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	### Urban Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = one }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.75 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = two }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = three }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.75 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.85 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = four }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.025 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.025 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.85 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.9 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = five }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.95 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.95 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = six }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.025 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.025 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = seven }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.9 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = eight }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = nine }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = ten }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 0.6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = eleven }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_popularity = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 0.25 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.45 }

	#Prevents modifiers from stacking endlessly
	
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_plsr_popularity }

	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_vns_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_ep_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_autonomists_final_pop = RUS_state_autonomists_popularity }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_final_pop = RUS_state_federalists_popularity }

RUS_calculate_polling_averages = {
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_poll_votes = 0 }

	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_poll_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = 0 }
		
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_poll_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_poll_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_poll_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		RUS_set_state_poll_votes_to_final_pop = yes
		RUS_multiply_state_poll_votes_to_poll_vote_count = yes
		RUS_round_state_poll_votes = yes
		RUS_count_total_state_poll_votes = yes

	}	
		
	RUS_round_poll_votes = yes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	RUS_count_total_poll_votes = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = RUS_pp_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	}
		
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_election_1936 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_pp_poll_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_pp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_pp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_pp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_monarchists_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_monarchists_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_pp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_autonomists_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_federalists_poll_votes  }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_monarchists_poll_votes  }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_rpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }

RUS_get_regional_senators = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_psr_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_pp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_vns_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_ep_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_independent_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_oblastniki_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_autonomists_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_federalists_state_senate_votes }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes > RUS_monarchists_state_senate_votes }			
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_state_regional_vote = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes > RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes }

	round_variable = RUS_federalists_state_presidential_votes
	round_variable = RUS_monarchists_state_presidential_votes
	
	
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_presidential_votes < 0 }	}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_pp_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_rovs_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_rovs_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_presidential_votes < 0 } }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {

	}

	round_variable = RUS_pp_state_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes

	round_variable = RUS_ep_state_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rovs_state_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes

	round_variable = RUS_autonomists_state_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_federalists_state_poll_votes

	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_pp_presidential_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_vns_presidential_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_ep_presidential_votes }

	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_autonomists_presidential_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_federalists_presidential_votes  }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes }

RUS_run_election = {
	RUS_clear_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		RUS_set_state_votes_to_final_pop = yes
		RUS_multiply_state_votes_to_vote_count = yes
		RUS_round_state_votes = yes
		RUS_count_total_state_votes = yes
		
		RUS_reset_temp_pop = yes
		
	}
	
	RUS_round_votes = yes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned  }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { 
				has_country_flag = pp_banned 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	RUS_count_total_votes = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_pp_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	}
		
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		log = "PLSR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_plsr_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		log = "NSP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nsp_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		log = "PSR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_psr_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
		log = "RSDRP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_rsdrp_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_kdp_votes }
			log = "KDP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_kdp_votes]"
			set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_pp_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
			log = "LKDP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_lkdp_votes]"
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_pp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_pp_votes }
			log = "PP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_pp_votes]"
			set_variable = { RUS_pp_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
			log = "RKDP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_rkdp_votes]"
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
		log = "VNS < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_vns_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
		log = "EP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_ep_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
		log = "NRPR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nrpr_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
		log = "NSNP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nsnp_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_monarchists_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_monarchists_votes }
		log = "RMS < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_monarchists_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_votes = 0 }
	}
		
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_plsr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_psr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_percentage_vote = RUS_kdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_vote = RUS_pp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_vns_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_ep_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_independent_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_percentage_vote = RUS_autonomists_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_percentage_vote = RUS_federalists_votes  }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_percentage_vote = RUS_monarchists_votes  }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_kdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_autonomists_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_federalists_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_monarchists_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^1 = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^2 = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^3 = RUS_psr_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^4 = RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote }
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = RUS_kdp_percentage_vote }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
		add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^3 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_vote }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^7 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^5 = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^6 = RUS_pp_percentage_vote }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^7 = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { RUS_russian_monarch = no }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_monarchists_percentage_vote }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^10 = RUS_monarchists_percentage_vote }
	}
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^8 = RUS_vns_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^9 = RUS_ep_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^11 = RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote }
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		add_to_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^3 = RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^12 = RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote }
	}
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^15 = RUS_independent_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^13 = RUS_autonomists_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^14 = RUS_federalists_percentage_vote }
	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = seats
		index = i

		multiply_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^i = 550 }
		round_variable = Duma_Party_Seats^i
	}
	
	set_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = seats
		index = i
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = Duma_Party_Seats^i }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 550 } }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 550 }
		subtract_from_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^15 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
	}
	
	set_variable = { plsr_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^1 }
	set_variable = { nsp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^2 }
	set_variable = { psr_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^3 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^4 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^5 }
	set_variable = { pp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^6 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^7 }
	set_variable = { vns_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^8 }
	set_variable = { ep_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^9 }
	set_variable = { monarchists_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^10  }
	set_variable = { nsnp_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^11 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { autonomists_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^13 }
	set_variable = { federalists_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^14  }
	set_variable = { independent_mp = Duma_Party_Seats^15 }
	
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_PLSR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NSP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_RSDRP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_PSR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_LKDP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_PP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_RKDP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_VNS_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_EP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NRPR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NSNP_CAMPAIGN
	round_variable = RUS_total_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR([?Duma_Party_Seats^1]) - NSP([?Duma_Party_Seats^2]) - RSDRP([?Duma_Party_Seats^4]) - PSR([?Duma_Party_Seats^3]) - LKDP([?lkdp_mp]) - RKDP([?rkdp_mp]) - VNS([?Duma_Party_Seats^8])"
	log = "EP([?Duma_Party_Seats^9]) - NRPR([?Duma_Party_Seats^12]) - NSNP([?Duma_Party_Seats^11]) - IND([?Duma_Party_Seats^15]) - AUT([?Duma_Party_Seats^13]) - FED ([?Duma_Party_Seats^14]) - RMS([?Duma_Party_Seats^10])"
	for_each_loop ={
		array = Duma_Party_Identity
		value = status
		index = i
		
		# Calculating total support
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 2 } 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^i < 1 }
						check_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i < 1 }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
	every_owned_state = { RUS_set_new_popularities_after_election = yes } 
}
RUS_find_the_election_winner = {
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = v
		index = i		
	}
	log = "[?i] becomes Winner with [?v]"
}
RUS_run_senate_election = {
	RUS_clear_senate_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_senate_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
		
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes
		
		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }
		
		RUS_set_state_senate_votes_to_final_pop = yes
		RUS_multiply_state_senate_votes_to_vote_count = yes
		RUS_round_state_senate_votes = yes
		RUS_count_total_state_senate_votes = yes
		
		#RUS_get_regional_senators = yes
		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_autonomists_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_federalists_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_monarchists_temp_pop = 0 }		
	}
	RUS_round_senate_votes = yes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { 
				has_country_flag = pp_banned 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	RUS_count_total_senate_votes = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_senate_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_votes = RUS_pp_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_pp_senate_regional_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_regional_votes }
	}
	# If below 5% fuck off (only for General Senate Elections, not regional!)
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = RUS_plsr_senate_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }

			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }

			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}

		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
