RUS_run_presidential_elections = {
	RUS_clear_president_election_variables = yes
	set_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_presidential_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_presidential_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_presidential_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_presidential_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		RUS_set_state_presidential_votes_to_final_pop = yes
		RUS_multiply_state_presidential_votes_to_presidential_vote_count = yes
		RUS_round_state_presidential_votes = yes
		RUS_count_total_state_presidential_votes = yes
		
		RUS_reset_temp_pop = yes
		
	}
	
	RUS_round_presidential_votes = yes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = pp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	RUS_count_total_presidential_votes = yes
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_plsr_presidential_votes }
		log = "PLSR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_plsr_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_nsp_presidential_votes }
		log = "NSP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nsp_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_psr_presidential_votes }
		log = "PSR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_psr_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes }
		log = "RSDRP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes }
		log = "LKDP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_pp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_pp_presidential_votes }
		log = "PP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_pp_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_pp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes }
		log = "RKDP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes]"

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_vns_presidential_votes }

		set_variable = { RUS_vns_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_ep_presidential_votes }
		log = "EP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_ep_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes }
		log = "NRPR < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes }
		log = "NSNP < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_presidential_votes = RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes }
		log = "RMS < [?RUS_temp_parliament_barrier] with [?RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes]"
		set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes = 0 }
	}
		
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_plsr_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_nsp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_psr_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_rsdrp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_kdp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_lkdp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_pp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_rkdp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_vns_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_ep_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_nrpr_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_nsnp_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_independent_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_autonomists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_autonomists_presidential_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_federalists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_federalists_presidential_votes  }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_monarchists_presidential_votes  }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_kdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_autonomists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_federalists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_monarchists_percentage_presidential_vote = RUS_total_presidential_votes }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_plsr_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }

	if = {

			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }

			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }

			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }

			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rkdp_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_vns_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_ep_president_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_vns_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_plsr_percentage_presidential_vote }

			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_psr_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_rsdrp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_lkdp_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_pp_percentage_presidential_vote }

			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_ep_percentage_presidential_vote }
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_presidential_vote > RUS_nrpr_percentage_presidential_vote }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsnp_president_victory
	}		
	round_variable = RUS_total_presidential_votes
	every_owned_state = { RUS_set_new_popularities_after_election = yes } 
}

mp_support_calc = {
	# 0 for Inactive, 1 for Governing, 2 for Supporting Government, 3 for Opposition, 4 for Sit-out
	# NOTE: Because of how arrays start at zero, the ID's for each party here are one less than normal
	set_variable = { mp_support = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = { plsr_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^1 = 1 } # PLSR  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { nsp_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^2 = 1 } # NSP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { psr_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^3 = 1 } # PSR  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { rsdrp_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^4 = 1 } # RSDRP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				lkdp_in_power = yes 
				AND = {
					kdp_in_power = yes
					has_country_flag = kdp_united
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^5 = 1 } # LKDP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { pp_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^6 = 1 } # PP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { rkdp_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^7 = 1 } # RKDP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { vns_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^8 = 1 } # VNS  (Governing)		
			}
	if = {
		limit = { ep_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^9 = 1 } # EP  (Governing)		
		}
	if = {
		limit = { nsnp_in_power = yes }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^11 = 1 } # NSNP  (Governing)		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo }
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^12 = 1 } # NRPR  (Governing)		
	}
	for_each_loop ={
		array = Duma_Party_Identity
		value = status
		index = i
		
		# Calculating total support
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 1 } 
					check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 2 } 
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { mp_support = Duma_Party_Seats^i }
		}
		# Setting Opposition
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 1 } }
				NOT = {	check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 2 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Duma_Party_Identity^i < 12 }
				}
				set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 3 }
			}
		}
		# Setting Sit-out
		else = {
			set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 4 }
		}
		# Setting as non-existing if have no seats
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { Duma_Party_Seats^i < 1 } 
					check_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i < 1 }
				} 
			}
			set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 0 }
		}
	}
}
senators_support_calc = {
	final_senators_recalc = yes	
	set_variable = { senate_support = 0 }
	for_each_loop ={
		array = Duma_Party_Identity
		value = status
		index = i
		
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 1 } 
				check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 2 } 
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { senate_support = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i }
		}
	}
}
final_senators_recalc = {
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^1 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^1 } 
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^2 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^2 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^3 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^4 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^4 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^5 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^5 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^7 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^7 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^8 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^8 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^9 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^9 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^10 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^10 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^11 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^11 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^12 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^12 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^13 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^13 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^14 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^14 }
	set_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_General_Seats^15 }
	
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^1 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^1 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^2 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^2 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^3 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^4 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^4 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^5 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^5 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^7 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^7 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^8 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^8 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^9 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^9 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^10 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^10 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^11 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^11 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^12 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^12 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^13 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^13 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^14 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^14 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_Regional_Seats^15 }
	
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^1 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^1 } 
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^2 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^2 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^3 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^4 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^4 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^5 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^5 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^7 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^7 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^8 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^8 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^9 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^9 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^10 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^10 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^11 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^11 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^12 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^12 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^13 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^13 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^14 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^14 }
	add_to_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^15 = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^15 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Senate_Party_Total_Seats
		value = seats
		index = i
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i }
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 150 } }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 150 }
		subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_Total_Seats^15 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
		subtract_from_variable = { Senate_Party_General_Seats^15 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
	}
}

RUS_increase_ruling_party_pop = {
	if = {
		limit = { plsr_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_plsr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { nsp_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_nsp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { psr_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_psr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { rsdrp_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_rsdrp_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { lkdp_in_power = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
			RUS_increase_kdp_pop = yes
		}
		else = {
			RUS_increase_lkdp_pop = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { pp_in_power = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
			RUS_increase_kdp_pop = yes
		}
		else = {
			RUS_increase_pp_pop = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { rkdp_in_power = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = kdp_united }
			RUS_increase_kdp_pop = yes
		}
		else = {
			RUS_increase_rkdp_pop = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { vns_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_vns_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ep_in_power = yes }
		RUS_increase_ep_pop = yes
	}
	if = {

RUS_decrease_plsr_pop_small = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_decrease_plsr_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = -0.025 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0.005 }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.035
		}
	}
}
RUS_decrease_nsp_pop_small = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_decrease_nsp_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = -0.025 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0.005 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_totalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = -0.035
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_psp
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = -0.035
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.035
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = -0.005 }

		if = {

			}
		}

				popularity = 0.035
			}
		}

RUS_increase_nsp_pop_large = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_nsp_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = -0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = -0.02 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_totalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_psp
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_increase_plsr_pop_election = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_plsr_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable_to_random = {
				var = pop_election
				min = 0.08
				max = 0.12
			}
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = pop_election }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = -0.01 }

RUS_increase_nsp_pop_election = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_nsp_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable_to_random = {
				var = pop_election
				min = 0.08
				max = 0.12
			}
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = pop_election }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_pp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = -0.01 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_totalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = RUS_nsp_is_psp
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}
		else = {

				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
		}

RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = {
	# Generate partial sums t1 = (P1), t2 = (P1 + P2), t3 = (P1 + P2 + P3)
	
	# so that we can use resize_array to fill our array with the right number of seats for each party
	set_temp_variable = { t1 = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { t2 = Duma_Party_Seats^1 }
	set_temp_variable = { t3 = Duma_Party_Seats^2 }
	set_temp_variable = { t4 = Duma_Party_Seats^3 }
	set_temp_variable = { t5 = Duma_Party_Seats^4 }
	set_temp_variable = { t6 = Duma_Party_Seats^5 }
	set_temp_variable = { t7 = Duma_Party_Seats^6 }
	set_temp_variable = { t8 = Duma_Party_Seats^7 }
	set_temp_variable = { t9 = Duma_Party_Seats^8 }
	set_temp_variable = { t10 = Duma_Party_Seats^9 }
	set_temp_variable = { t11 = Duma_Party_Seats^10 }
	set_temp_variable = { t12 = Duma_Party_Seats^11 }
	set_temp_variable = { t13 = Duma_Party_Seats^12 }
	set_temp_variable = { t14 = Duma_Party_Seats^13 }
	set_temp_variable = { t15 = Duma_Party_Seats^14 }
	set_temp_variable = { t16 = 550 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = t1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t3 = t2 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t4 = t3 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t5 = t4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t6 = t5 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t7 = t6 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t8 = t7 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t9 = t8 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t10 = t9 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t11 = t10 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t12 = t11 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t13 = t12 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t14 = t13 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t15 = t14 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t16 = t15 }
	
	clear_array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
	
	# Resize array to t1 seats, setting P1 frame numbers to 1 (Party 1 color)
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 1 size = t1 }
	# Resize array to t2 seats, setting P2 frame numbers to 2 (Party 2 color)
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 2 size = t2 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 3 size = t3 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 4 size = t4 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 5 size = t5 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 6 size = t6 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 7 size = t7 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 8 size = t8 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 9 size = t9 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 10 size = t10 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 11 size = t11 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 12 size = t12 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 13 size = t13 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 14 size = t14 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 15 size = t15 }
	# Resize array to all 550 seats
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Lower_House_Display value = 16 size = t16 }
	
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: DUMA ARRAY LENGHT [?RUS_Lower_House_Display^num]"
}
RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = {
	# Generate partial sums t1 = (P1), t2 = (P1 + P2), t3 = (P1 + P2 + P3)
	
	# so that we can use resize_array to fill our array with the right number of seats for each party
	set_temp_variable = { t1 = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { t2 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^1 }
	set_temp_variable = { t3 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^2 }
	set_temp_variable = { t4 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^3 }
	set_temp_variable = { t5 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^4 }
	set_temp_variable = { t6 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^5 }
	set_temp_variable = { t7 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^6 }
	set_temp_variable = { t8 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^7 }
	set_temp_variable = { t9 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^8 }
	set_temp_variable = { t10 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^9 }
	set_temp_variable = { t11 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^10 }
	set_temp_variable = { t12 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^11 }
	set_temp_variable = { t13 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^12 }
	set_temp_variable = { t14 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^13 }
	set_temp_variable = { t15 = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^14 }
	set_temp_variable = { t16 = 150 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { t1 = t0 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = t1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t3 = t2 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t4 = t3 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t5 = t4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t6 = t5 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t7 = t6 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t8 = t7 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t9 = t8 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t10 = t9 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t11 = t10 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t12 = t11 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t13 = t12 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t14 = t13 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t15 = t14 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t16 = t15 }
	
	clear_array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
	
	# Resize array to t1 seats, setting P1 frame numbers to 1 (Party 1 color)
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 1 size = t1 }
	# Resize array to t2 seats, setting P2 frame numbers to 2 (Party 2 color)
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 2 size = t2 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 3 size = t3 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 4 size = t4 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 5 size = t5 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 6 size = t6 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 7 size = t7 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 8 size = t8 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 9 size = t9 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 10 size = t10 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 11 size = t11 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 12 size = t12 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 13 size = t13 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 14 size = t14 }
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 15 size = t15 }
	# Resize array to all 550 seats, setting remaining frame numbers to 16 (Party 16 color)
	resize_array = { array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display value = 16 size = t16 }
	
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: SENATE ARRAY LENGHT [?RUS_Senate_Election_Display^num]"
	set_variable = { three_fifth_of_senate = 90 }
}

predetermine_all_presidential_candidates = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = NSP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = PSR_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {	
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = EP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSNP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = NSNP_candidate_existed
	}
}
restore_all_presidential_candidates = {

	}

		limit = {

setup_presidential_government_senate = {
	RUS_decrease_ruling_party_pop_large = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_a_vns_president = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible }
			}
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			set_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = VNS_aristocratic }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = RUS_authoritarian_democrat_party
					long_name = RUS_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		RUS_setup_vns_government = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_a_ep_president = yes }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		RUS_increase_ep_pop_large = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				name = RUS_eurasianist_party
				long_name = RUS_eurasianist_party_long
			}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_hog_ade
			RUS_Georgiy_V_Vernadskiy_for_ade
			RUS_Konstantin_A_Chkheidze_eco_ade
			RUS_Pyetr_N_Savitskiy_sec_ade
		}
		set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^9 = 1 }	
		add_political_power = 100
		add_ideas = RUS_Eurasianism_Idea
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_alt } }
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
		}
		set_country_flag = disable_duma
		set_country_flag = RUS_duma_dissolved
		set_country_flag = RUS_DPROM
		hidden_effect = {
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			load_focus_tree = RUS_EURASIAN_UNION_FOCUS
		}
		RUS_remove_riga_accords = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.10
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_a_pp_president = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible }
			}
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			set_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		RUS_setup_progressive_government = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_a_rkdp_president = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible }
			}
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			set_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		RUS_setup_rkdp_government = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_a_lkdp_president = yes}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible }
			}
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			set_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		RUS_setup_lkdp_government = yes
	}	
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
}
setup_ruling_party_president = {
	clr_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_LKDP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_RKDP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_PLSR_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_NSP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_NSNP_Candidate_Winner
	restore_all_presidential_candidates = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				plsr_in_power = yes
				nsp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			psr_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = maklakov_psr_kdp_candidate
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			rsdrp_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			kdp_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_LKDP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_RKDP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
				NOT = { has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate }
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			vns_in_power = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			ep_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_EP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			nsnp_in_power = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_NSNP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	setup_new_president = yes
}
setup_new_president = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_vernadskiy = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_savitskiy = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = yusupov_vns_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = yusupov_vns_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_yusupov = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_romanov = yes
			}			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = maklakov_psr_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = maklakov_kdp_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_maklakov = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = teslenko_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate
					}		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_teslenko = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_tereschenko = yes
			}			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = gershtein_psr_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_gershtein = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = avksentiev_psr_candidate	
						has_country_flag = avksentiev_psr_kdp_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_avksentiev = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_chernov = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
			}
			RUS_setup_president_lozovskiy = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = gershtein_psr_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_gershtein = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_lozovskiy = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
			}
			RUS_setup_president_odinets = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_NSNP_Candidate_Winner
			}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = vergun_nsnp_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_vergun = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = trushnovich_nsnp_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_trushnovich = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = pryanishnikov_nsnp_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_pryanishnikov = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_georgievsky = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^28 = 3 } }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SENATE_NSP_REFORM_accepted }
			}
			remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
		}
	}
}
remove_add_presidential_senators = {
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_senate_seats_removed }
		}
		for_each_loop = {
			array = Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats
			value = seats
			index = i
			
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^i = 0 }
		}		
		if = {
			limit = { RUS_denikin_in_power = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^8 = 20 }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^15 = 30 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_vns_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^8 = 40 }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^9 = 5 }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^10 = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_ep_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^9 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_a_rkdp_president = yes
					has_a_pp_president = yes
					has_a_lkdp_president = yes
				}
				has_country_flag = kdp_united
			}
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^5 = 50 }		
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_a_rkdp_president = yes }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^7 = 50 }		
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_a_pp_president = yes }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^6 = 50 }		
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_a_lkdp_president = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_soclibs_rrdo }
					set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 50 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^5 = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_psr_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_rsdrp_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^4 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_nrpr_president = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 50 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^12 = 50 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_nsnp_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^11 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_nsp_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^2 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_a_plsr_president = yes }
			set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^1 = 50 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Pitirim Sorokin"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = democratic_block_coalition }
				}
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^8 = 20 }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 10 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = democratic_block_coalition
				}
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^5 = 15 }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^4 = 10 }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 25 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = RUS_I_Was_Never_A_Socialist
				}
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^5 = 40 }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 10 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = RUS_I_Was_Never_A_Liberal
				}
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^4 = 20 }
				set_variable = { Senate_Party_Presidential_Seats^3 = 30 }
			}		
		}
		
		final_senators_recalc = yes
		senators_support_calc = yes
		RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
	}
}

	add_ideas = var:RUS_plsr_minister_sec

		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition
		}
		RUS_rsdrp_supports_gov = yes
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^1 = 1 }
}

			name = RUS_rsrpi_party
			long_name = RUS_rsrpi_party_long
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = RUS_social_democrat_party
			long_name = RUS_social_democrat_party_long
		}
	}
	add_ideas = var:RUS_rsdrp_minister_hog
	add_ideas = var:RUS_rsdrp_minister_for
	add_ideas = var:RUS_rsdrp_minister_eco
	add_ideas = var:RUS_rsdrp_minister_sec
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
		RUS_add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = psr_coalition
		RUS_add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^4 = 1 }
}

		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^3 = 1 }
}

	add_ideas = var:RUS_vns_minister_eco

		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }

			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
				add_to_coalition = yes		
			}
		}
	}
	mp_support_calc = yes
	senators_support_calc = yes
	set_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^8 = 1 }
}

clear_previous_variables_for_legislation = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = support
		index = i
		
		set_variable = { CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i = 0 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Senate_Party_Total_Seats
		value = support
		index = i
		
		set_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i = 0 }
	}
}
RUS_LAW_calculate_support = {
	# Opposition votes AGAINST despite all
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Status
		value = status
		index = i
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^i = 3 } }
			set_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^i = 0 }
			set_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^i = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = support
		index = i
		
		set_variable = { CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i = Duma_Party_Seats^i }
		multiply_variable = { CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i = CurrentSupportForBillPerc^i }
		round_variable = CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i
		add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i }
	}	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Senate_Party_Total_Seats
		value = support
		index = i
		
		set_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i }
		multiply_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i = CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^i }
		round_variable = CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i
		add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i }
	}		
	
}
Get_initial_RUS_LAW_IMPEACH_PRESIDENT = {
	clear_previous_variables_for_legislation = yes
	
	# Initial Support #
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_vns_president = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.15 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.7 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_ep_president = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.75 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0.8 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.25 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.7 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0.75 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_lkdp_president = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0.8 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.25 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_a_rkdp_president = yes
				has_a_pp_president = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0.8 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.22 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_nsnp_president = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.85 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0.85 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_a_psr_president = yes
				has_a_rsdrp_president = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^6 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^7 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^8 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^9 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^7 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^8 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^9 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_a_plsr_president = yes
				has_a_nsp_president = yes
				has_a_socialist_president = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^5 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^6 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^7 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^8 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^9 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^5 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^7 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^8 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^9 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^1 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^2 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^3 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^4 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^6 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^7 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^8 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^1 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^2 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^3 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^4 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^5 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^7 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^8 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^9 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^12 = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^11 = 0 }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { CurrentSupportForBillPerc^15 = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { CurrentSenateSupportForBillPerc^15 = 0 }
	
	RUS_LAW_calculate_support = yes
	count_votes_for_bill_sum = yes 
}

Get_initial_RUS_LAW_PSR_NEW_CONST = {
	clear_previous_variables_for_legislation = yes
	
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Reassure_Unity_With_NRPR
		}
		# Initial Support #
		randomize_psr_support_average = yes
		randomize_ep_support_very_low = yes
		randomize_nrpr_support_high = yes
		randomize_independent_support_low = yes
	}
	else = {
		# Initial Support #
		randomize_plsr_support_very_low = yes
		randomize_nsp_support_low = yes
		randomize_psr_support_high = yes
		randomize_rsdrp_support_average = yes
		randomize_lkdp_support_high = yes
		randomize_nsnp_support_very_low = yes
		randomize_independent_support_low = yes
	}
	
	RUS_LAW_calculate_support = yes

count_votes_for_bill_sum = {
	set_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = 0 }
	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Duma_Party_Seats
		value = votes
		index = i
		
		clamp_variable = { var = CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i min = 0 max = Duma_Party_Seats^i }
		add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentDumaSupportForBill^i }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Senate_Party_Total_Seats
		value = votes
		index = i
		
		clamp_variable = { var = CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i min = 0 max = Senate_Party_Total_Seats^i }
		add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentSenateSupportForBill^i }
	}
	round_variable = CurrentOverallSupport
	round_variable = CurrentOverallSenateSupport 
	
}
RUS_pass_current_law = {
	set_variable = { RUS_law_in_progress = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^6 = 2 }
		}
		country_event = rusdem.374
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^7 = 2 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusdem.307
			days = 2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^8 = 2 }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_free_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_free_trade_unions
				add_idea = trade_unions_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = banned_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = banned_trade_unions
				add_idea = trade_unions_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_non_socialist_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_non_socialist_trade_unions
				add_idea = trade_unions_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
				add_idea = trade_unions_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = trade_unions_3
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_LAW_NATIONALIZATION_TRADE_UNIONS_tt
		add_to_variable = { RUS_NEP_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = -0.025 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_NEP_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.025 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_NEP_party_popularity_stability_factor = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = russoc.146
				days = 15
				random_days = 100
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^3 = 2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_PRESIDENT_WILL_BE_IMPEACHED
		country_event = rusdem.107
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^9 = 2}
		}
		country_event = rusdem.416
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^16 = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = banned_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = banned_trade_unions
				add_idea = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_non_socialist_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_non_socialist_trade_unions
				add_idea = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_free_trade_unions }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_free_trade_unions
				add_idea = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
		}	
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^17 = 2 }
		}
		add_ideas = RUS_cheap_housing
		add_ideas = social_security		
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25
		RUS_increase_psr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^19 = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_industrial_zones
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_industrial_zones
				add_idea = RUS_state_regulation
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_New_Economic_Policy_modifier }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_nep_increase_state
			add_to_variable = { RUS_nep_market = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_nep_state = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_modify_nep	
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_NEP_consumer_goods_factor = 0.08
				tooltip = consumer_goods_factor_tooltip
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_NEP_industrial_capacity_factory = 0.04
				tooltip = industrial_capacity_factory_tooltip
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_NEP_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = 0.03
				tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tooltip
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_NEP_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = 0.05
				tooltip = production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor_tooltip
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^20 = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = social_security
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = social_security
				add_idea = RUS_fair_labour
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = RUS_fair_labour
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^21 = 2 }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.12
		}

			set_variable = { Duma_Bill_Status^i = 4 } # Fail
		}
	}

}

clear_law_country_flag = {
	clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_OPPOSITION_VOTES
	set_variable = { RUS_law_in_progress = 0 }
	clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_CHANGING_CONSTITUTION
	
}
fire_notification_for_player_law = {
	#fire notification if player
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_ai = no }
				NOT = { is_in_array = { FROM.duma_bills_alerts = law_id } }
			}
			add_to_array = { FROM.duma_bills_alerts = law_id }
			FROM = { scoped_sound_effect = duma_sfx }
			set_variable_to_random = global.kaiserreich_alerts_dirty
		}
	}
}

	activate_mission = RUS_petrograd_campaigning
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = rusdem.250
			days = 95
			random_days = 10
		}
	}
}
